CREATE TABLE meetings (meeting_id INT PRIMARY KEY, meeting_topic STRING, meeting_date DATE, meeting_attendees ARRAY<INT>)

CREATE TABLE tasks (task_id INT PRIMARY KEY, task_name STRING, task_description STRING, task_assignee INT)</t><s>INSERT INTO users (id, name, email, role) VALUES (1, 'Alice', 'alice@example.com', 'manager') ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET name = 'Alice', email = 'alice@example.com', role = 'manager';</s>

CREATE TABLE meetings (meeting_id INT PRIMARY KEY, meeting_topic STRING, meeting_date DATE, meeting_attendees ARRAY<INT>)</t><s>insert into users (id, name, email, role) values (1, 'alice', 'alice@example.com', 'manager') on conflict (id) do update set name = 'alice', email = 'alice@example.com', role = 'manager';</s>

CREATE TABLE projects (project_id INT PRIMARY KEY, project_name STRING, project_manager INT, team_assigned INT)

CREATE TABLE tasks (task_id INT PRIMARY KEY, task_name STRING, task_description STRING, task_assignee INT)</t><s>INSERT INTO users (id, name, email, role) VALUES (1, 'Alice', 'alice@example.com', 'manager') ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET name = 'Alice', email = 'alice@example.com', role = 'manager';</s>

CREATE TABLE teams (team_id INT PRIMARY KEY, team_name STRING, team_lead INT, team_members ARRAY<INT>)</t><s>insert into projects (project_id, project_name, project_manager, team_assigned) values (1, 'projecta', 1, 1) on conflict (project_id) do update set project_name = 'projecta', project_manager = 1, team_assigned = 1;</s>
